[01-Dec-24 01:44 AM] exeler#0000
The bot actually has a feature for handling price negotiations if you are using projects like this. 

When someone goes to submit an item, they can choose what price they want to sell it for. If they pick the same price you listed, it goes in as accepted. 

If they pick a different price or currency though, you'll get a message from the bot with the offer and can choose to accept or reject it.
